if (is_file('setup/setup_base.css') && (sha1_file('setup/setup_base.css') != '4c6791d83aa61ea9d1bfee66f4663c2c0a7b6c07')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/setup_base.css');
	$tmp = pathinfo('setup/setup_base.css');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/setup_base.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('setup/setup_base.css', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_3();
if (!is_file('setup/setup_base.css')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/setup_base.css');
} else if (sha1_file('setup/setup_base.css') != '4c6791d83aa61ea9d1bfee66f4663c2c0a7b6c07') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/setup_base.css');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/setup_base.css', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/setup_base.css');
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'fdefa006d6d36939c941a6e429c175c4a890756d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'fdefa006d6d36939c941a6e429c175c4a890756d') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '3f4432b8622b0d54402b22cd752264d004edbac9') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'fdefa006d6d36939c941a6e429c175c4a890756d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}

		writefile_6();

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('update/check.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('update/check.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('update/check.php') !== '26fdd647c81a402ce195642bd26806dd30311ec2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): update/check.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: update/index.php');
	writefile_11();
	if (!is_file('update/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): update/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('update/index.php') != 'ae329162a41ac57f6ff7c39f04343b8d1cc7a097') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('update/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of update/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== 'ae329162a41ac57f6ff7c39f04343b8d1cc7a097') {
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== '4f0276d3255f9ccdd9c7c682f593cf0c777251da') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: update/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('update/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('update/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('update/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_11();
		if (@sha1_file('update/index.php') !== 'ae329162a41ac57f6ff7c39f04343b8d1cc7a097') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): update/index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('userdata/info.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: userdata/info.txt');
	writefile_12();
	if (!is_file('userdata/info.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): userdata/info.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('userdata/info.txt') != '4dba9a327ba948d5681a281997cf877006e5689b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): userdata/info.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('userdata/info.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of userdata/info.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('userdata/info.txt') !== '4dba9a327ba948d5681a281997cf877006e5689b') {
		if (@sha1_file('userdata/info.txt') !== '14c2381fb12b7b7d58ce1ff3aa93c060c72aa393') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: userdata/info.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('userdata/info.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('userdata/info.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('userdata/info.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('userdata/info.txt') !== '4dba9a327ba948d5681a281997cf877006e5689b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): userdata/info.txt');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File could not be deleted: setup/setup.css');
}

	warn('File could not be deleted: setup/setup.js.php');
}
